【第二百八十八題 / NO. 288】


Universal Containers wants to implement a customer verification process where sensitive account information can only be accessed after the customer passes identity verification. The agent must enforce this security rule deterministically without allowing the large language model (LLM) to bypass the verification requirement.
What should an Agentforce Specialist recommend as the best solution?


Universal Containers 希望實施客戶驗證流程，只有在客戶通過身分驗證後才能存取敏感帳戶資訊。Agent 必須確定性地強制執行此安全規則，而不允許大型語言模型 (LLM) 繞過驗證要求。
Agentforce 專家應推薦什麼作為最佳解決方案？


A. Use context variables to store verification status in the messaging session and configure the agent to check these variables through natural language prompts during each sensitive action.

使用上下文變數在訊息工作階段中儲存驗證狀態，並設定 Agent 在每個敏感動作期間透過自然語言提示檢查這些變數。

B. Include detailed verification instructions in the agent's topic instructions explaining when customers should be verified and rely on the LLM to follow these guidelines consistently across all interactions.

在 Agent 的主題指令中包含詳細的驗證說明，解釋何時應驗證客戶，並依賴 LLM 在所有互動中一致地遵循這些準則。

C. Create a custom variable IsCustomerVerified set by a verification action, then apply a conditional filter using the expression IsCustomerVerified equals true to all sensitive data actions, ensuring deterministic access control that the LLM can't alter.

建立一個由驗證動作設定的自訂變數 IsCustomerVerified，然後對所有敏感資料動作套用條件篩選器，使用運算式 IsCustomerVerified 等於 true，以確保 LLM 無法更改的確定性存取控制。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The AgentForce Security and Deterministic Logic Guide specifies that sensitive actions must be gated through conditional filters linked to verification variables, not through natural language... This configuration ensures security and determinism because the execution of sensitive actions is programmatically enforced.

為了實現「確定性」和「安全」的控制，不能依賴 LLM 的判斷（選項 A 和 B）。必須使用系統層級的邏輯控制：設定一個變數來追蹤驗證狀態，並在敏感動作上加上「條件篩選器 (Conditional Filter)」。這樣，只有當變數確認已驗證時，動作才會被系統允許執行，完全排除了 LLM 繞過規則的可能性。

【第二百八十九題 / NO. 289】


Universal Containers (UC) is using Einstein Generative AI to generate an account summary. UC aims to ensure the content is safe and inclusive, utilizing the Einstein Trust Layer's toxicity scoring to assess the content's safety level.
In the Einstein Generative AI Toxicity Scoring system, what does a toxicity score of 1 indicate?


Universal Containers (UC) 正在使用 Einstein 生成式 AI 來生成帳戶摘要。UC 旨在確保內容安全且具包容性，利用 Einstein 信任層的毒性評分來評估內容的安全級別。
在 Einstein 生成式 AI 毒性評分系統中，毒性分數為 1 代表什麼？


A. The response is the least toxic.

回應是毒性最小的。

B. The response is not toxic.

回應沒有毒性。

C. The response is the most toxic.

回應是毒性最大的。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Einstein Trust Layer's Toxicity Scoring categorizes content on a scale of 0 to 1, where 1 indicates the highest level of toxicity (e.g., harmful, biased, or inappropriate language).

在毒性評分系統中，分數範圍是 0 到 1。0 代表無毒性（安全），而 1 代表「最高毒性」（極度有害或不適當）。這與「安全類別分數」不同（在那裡 1 可能代表安全，具體取決於上下文），但在直接的毒性評分中，1 是最糟的情況。

【第二百九十題 / NO. 290】


An Agentforce at Universal Containers is trying to set up a new Field Generation prompt template. They take the following steps.
1. Create a new Field Generation prompt template.
2. Choose Case as the object type.
3. Select the custom field AI_Analysis_c as the target field.
After creating the prompt template, the Agentforce Specialist saves, tests, and activates it. Howsoever, when they go to a case record, the AI Analysis field does not show the (Sparkle) icon on the Edit pencil. When the Agentforce Specialist was editing the field, it was behaving as a normal field.
Which critical step did the Agentforce Specialist miss?


Universal Containers 的一位 Agentforce 人員正試圖設定一個新的欄位生成提示範本。他們採取了以下步驟。
1. 建立一個新的欄位生成提示範本。
2. 選擇 Case 作為物件類型。
3. 選擇自訂欄位 AI_Analysis_c 作為目標欄位。
建立提示範本後，Agentforce 專家儲存、測試並啟用了它。但是，當他們進入個案記錄時，AI Analysis 欄位在編輯鉛筆上沒有顯示（閃光）圖示。當 Agentforce 專家編輯該欄位時，它的行為就像一個普通欄位。
Agentforce 專家錯過了哪個關鍵步驟？


A. They forgot to reactivate the Lightning page layout for the Case object after activating their Field Generation prompt template.

他們忘記在啟用欄位生成提示範本後重新啟用 Case 物件的 Lightning 頁面版面配置。

B. They forgot that the Case Object is not supported for Add generation as Feinstein Service Replies should be used instead.

他們忘記 Case 物件不支援新增生成，應改用 Einstein 服務回覆。

C. They forgot to edit the Lightning page layout and associate the field to a prompt template

他們忘記編輯 Lightning 頁面版面配置並將欄位關聯到提示範本。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
For Field Generation prompt templates to display the Sparkle icon (indicating AI-generated content), the target field must be explicitly associated with the prompt template on the Lightning page layout.

僅僅建立並啟用提示範本是不夠的。必須在「Lightning 應用程式建構器 (Lightning App Builder)」中，編輯包含該欄位的頁面，選中該欄位，並在屬性面板中明確選擇要使用的提示範本。這一步驟將範本與 UI 綁定，才會顯示 AI 生成圖示。

【第二百九十一題 / NO. 291】


When a verified customer in a help center says, "I want to upgrade my service plan," an AI agent needs to complete the following tasks:
* Verify identity and entitlement.
* Create a new quote.
* Calculate a prorated upgrade amount.
* Escalate to an Account Executive (AE) only if the reorder exceeds USD 25,000.
Which type of agent should an AgentForce Specialist build to support this use case?


當一位已驗證的客戶在說明中心說：「我想升級我的服務計劃」時，AI Agent 需要完成以下任務：
* 驗證身分和權利。
* 建立新的報價。
* 計算按比例分配的升級金額。
* 僅當重新訂購超過 25,000 美元時，才升級給客戶經理 (AE)。
AgentForce 專家應建立哪種類型的 Agent 來支援此使用案例？


A. Service Agent to resolve the case end-to-end and create a new opportunity for the sales team

服務 Agent，以端對端解決個案並為銷售團隊建立新機會

B. Sales Agent to handle the upsell and large-deal escalation

銷售 Agent，以處理追加銷售和大額交易升級

C. Employee Agent to orchestrate internal logistics and finance

員工 Agent，以協調內部物流和財務

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
This scenario represents a revenue-generating interaction where the AI agent is directly handling an upsell process. The tasks include verifying the customer's entitlement, generating a new quote, and calculating a prorated amount - all of which align with the Sales Agent configuration type in AgentForce.

這個場景的核心是「追加銷售 (Upsell)」和「報價管理 (Quote Management)」。雖然發生在說明中心，但涉及的業務邏輯（建立報價、計算金額、大額交易升級）都屬於銷售範疇。Agentforce 的「銷售 Agent (Sales Agent)」專為處理這類創收互動、報價生成和交易升級而設計。相比之下，服務 Agent 更側重於故障排除和支援工單。

【第二百九十二題 / NO. 292】


Universal Containers' data science team is hosting a generative large language model (LLM) on Amazon Web Services (AWS).
What should the team use to access externally-hosted models in the Salesforce Platform?


Universal Containers 的資料科學團隊正在 Amazon Web Services (AWS) 上託管一個生成式大型語言模型 (LLM)。
團隊應該使用什麼來存取 Salesforce 平台中的外部託管模型？


A. Model Builder

模型產生器 (Model Builder)

B. App Builder

應用程式建構器 (App Builder)

C. Copilot Builder

Copilot 建構器

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
To access externally-hosted models, such as a large language model (LLM) hosted on AWS, the Model Builder in Salesforce is the appropriate tool. Model Builder allows teams to integrate and deploy external AI models into the Salesforce platform.

Einstein Studio 中的「模型產生器 (Model Builder)」是 Salesforce 連接外部 AI 世界的橋樑。它支援「自帶模型 (Bring Your Own Model, BYOM)」架構，允許企業將託管在 AWS、Google Cloud 或 Databricks 等外部平台上的模型（包括生成式 LLM）註冊並整合到 Salesforce 中，使其能夠像原生模型一樣被 Flow、Apex 或 Prompt Builder 調用。
